<Review>I don't think I've ever experienced so many unique and delicious flavors all in one spot. The "Night Vision" cocktail caught my EYE and was very good! It was not too carrot-y or gingery as our waiter promised.

AMBIANCE is lovely, with low lighting, small tables, fresh plants and whimsical turnips on their wall. SERVICE was excellent also, from the waiter to the food runners, everyone was friendly and professional.

FOOD was the best part. They gave us some complimentary grilled radishes -- yummy -- who knew? We also had their bok choy dish with pickled veggies, sweet potato app which was delectable, and last but not least, their hand torn pasta - a must try! The pasta was delicate and their peas with cream sauce and herbs created a perfectly balanced dish that didn't leave you feeling weighed down. The plates are good for sharing and 3-4 for 2 people is plenty.

Ah, I almost forgot about dessert. We saved some room for dessert and per the waiter's recommendation, ordered the peanut butter pudding, which was different than I thought and underwhelming for me. Wouldn't order it again.

I would definitely like to try one of their few sister restaurants on the block next time!<//Review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN2Nrt1tIZekTpHfVY4H2Rhi2NaCgpzbcceg9ay=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPyXWCtYiz1w6-cY43KVHrU9rtdDEIuBawbM3Vo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMRlLpn4WgPkw4fuRB2xRdr7nzrY4-nyCLRlUZY=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMj3N1mYp_nT9sTbj0Orz2j5WvfKJ1d5ywh1hE2=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNZZfKYQyBBYu0P7YQJblfdaUVG3QNFe4WDl6y5=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pictures>< GmapID>

< review>
So... You're vegan and your date is a carnivore(your problems are far deeper than looking for a place to eat). Here is your veg friendly choice. I know it's difficult to find places like this, but with PYT, you don't really need to go anywhere else. Make a rezzie, park on the street (unlikely but worth a couple of laps around the block) or in the lot on the other side of Main street,  and enjoy this quaint space.
The bar has crafted drinks and a solid wine selection. The lighting is romantic. The service is courteous and menu savvy.  Speaking of the menu, you really can't go wrong. It's all organic and locally sourced.
A great date joint in the heart of downtown LA.<//review>

< review>
Their Mexican pastries are the best and most authentic I've tasted. When we're craving sweet bread, we go out of our way to buy from them. Their staff is courteous and they have something for all tastes. My favorite, for the moment, is a sweet vanilla cream filled pastry with a delicate sugar paste on the outside. First time here since Maki Yaki closed and we decided to try Fat Belly Grill for lunch. We odered the chicken teriyaki bowl and the weekly special.
It took 20 minutes to get our food after we ordered. The chicken was room temperature and vegtables were still slightly frozen. The only thing hot was the rice. I received two pieces of "chicken breast" that looked the exact same making me think they use frozen processed chicken.(Look at the picture they have of their chicken teriyaki bento box).  Also when we were leaving two other people who were there before us were asking for their lunch to go since it took so long to get their food they were going to be "late getting back to work." They had only received their Miso soups at that time. I'll also add there was a maximum of 6 people dining in at the time of our visit.

I hate to say it but I'd rather go to Flame Broiler than go back to Fat Belly Grill due to service and food quality.<//text>
